 131 | class SwitchboardActionPayload(BaseModel):
 132 |     action_key: str
 133 |     payload: Dict[str, Any]
 134 | 
 135 | @router.post("/switchboard/execute-action")
 136 | async def execute_switchboard_action(
 137 |     req: SwitchboardActionPayload,
 138 |     db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)
 139 | ):
 140 |     """
 141 |     @description: Universal action dispatcher for the Switchboard. 
 142 |     The frontend sends an intent, the backend decides what it means.
 143 |     """
 144 |     action = req.action_key
 145 |     data = req.payload
 146 |     
 147 |     if action == "TOGGLE_ACTIVE":
 148 |         binding_id = data.get("id")
 149 |         current_state = data.get("is_active", True)
 150 |         update_payload = PolicyBindingUpdate(is_active=not current_state)
 151 |         await MetaService.update_binding(db, binding_id, update_payload)
 152 |         return {"status": "success", "message": "Enforcement toggled"}
 153 |         
 154 |     elif action == "DELETE_BINDING":
 155 |         binding_id = data.get("id")
 156 |         await MetaService.delete_binding(db, binding_id)
 157 |         return {"status": "success", "message": "Jurisdiction removed"}
 158 |         
 159 |     raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"Unknown Action: {action}")
 160 |

 223 | @router.get("/domains")
 224 | async def list_domains(db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)):
 225 |     # 1. Dynamic Domains from DB (The "Wild" Ones)
 226 |     result = await db.execute(select(distinct(AttributeDefinition.domain)))
 227 |     dynamic_domains = result.scalars().all()
 228 |     
 229 |     # 2. System Domains from Registry (The "Official" Ones)
 230 |     registered_domains = await domain_registry.get_all_summaries(db)
 231 |     
 232 |     # 3. Merge Strategy
 233 |     domain_map = {}
 234 |     
 235 |     # A. Add Registered Domains (Source of Truth)
 236 |     for d in registered_domains:
 237 |         data = d.model_dump()
 238 |         domain_map[data["key"]] = {
 239 |             "key": data["key"],
 240 |             "label": data["label"],
 241 |             "type": data["type"],
 242 |             "type_def": data["type_def"], 
 243 |             "system_module": data.get("system_module", "GENERAL"),
 244 |             "module_label": data.get("module_label", "General"),
 245 |             "module_icon": data.get("module_icon", "antd:AppstoreOutlined"),
 246 |             "icon": data.get("icon"),
 247 |             "parent": data.get("parent_domain"),
 248 |             "scopes": data["scopes"]
 249 |         }
 250 |         
 251 |     # B. Add Dynamic Domains (if any found that aren't registered)
 252 |     for d_key in dynamic_domains:
 253 |         if d_key not in domain_map:
 254 |             domain_map[d_key] = {
 255 |                 "key": d_key,
 256 |                 "label": d_key.replace('_', ' ').title(),
 257 |                 "type": "STANDARD", 
 258 |                 "system_module": "DYNAMIC", 
 259 |                 "module_label": "Dynamic Data",
 260 |                 "module_icon": "antd:DatabaseOutlined",
 261 |                 "icon": "antd:DatabaseOutlined",
 262 |                 "parent": None,
 263 |                 "scopes": [{"key": "DEFAULT", "label": "Default Scope", "type": "CONTAINER"}]
 264 |             }
 265 | 
 266 |     return list(domain_map.values())

   6 | from sqlalchemy.orm import DeclarativeBase
   7 | 
   8 | class Base(DeclarativeBase):
   9 |     """
  10 |     The shared registry for all database models.
  11 |     All Domain Models and Kernel Models must inherit from this.
  12 |     """
  13 |     pass
  14 | 
  15 | # --- NOTE ON MIGRATIONS ---
  16 | # Alembic's env.py handles the discovery of models dynamically.
  17 | # We do NOT need to import them here. Doing so causes circular imports
  18 | # because models need to import 'Base' from this file first.

# Source code from: backend\app\core\database\session.py
----------------------------------------------------------
   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/database/session.py
   2 | # @file: Async Database Engine
   3 | # @author: The Engineer
   4 | # @description: Configures the SQLAlchemy Async Engine and Session Factory.
   5 | # This is the "Heart" that pumps data to the API.
   6 | # UPDATED: Logging disabled (echo=False) for performance.
   7 | 
   8 | from typing import AsyncGenerator
   9 | 
  10 | from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import create_async_engine, async_sessionmaker, AsyncSession
  11 | from app.core.config import settings
  12 | 
  13 | # 1. Configure Connection Arguments
  14 | # SQLite requires specific flags to handle async threads correctly.
  15 | # Postgres does not need this.
  16 | connect_args = {}
  17 | if "sqlite" in settings.DATABASE_URL:
  18 |     connect_args["check_same_thread"] = False
  19 | 
  20 | # 2. Create the Async Engine (The Connection Pool)
  21 | engine = create_async_engine(
  22 |     settings.DATABASE_URL,
  23 |     echo=False,                # âš¡ PERFORMANCE: Logging disabled based on Directive P2-S3
  24 |     future=True,
  25 |     connect_args=connect_args,
  26 | )
  27 | 
  28 | # 3. Create the Session Factory
  29 | # This generates short-lived "sessions" for each API request.
  30 | AsyncSessionLocal = async_sessionmaker(
  31 |     bind=engine,
  32 |     class_=AsyncSession,
  33 |     autoflush=False,
  34 |     expire_on_commit=False,
  35 | )
  36 | 
  37 | # 4. Dependency Injection (The "Needle")
  38 | # Endpoints use this to get a safe, isolated database session.
  39 | async def get_db() -> AsyncGenerator[AsyncSession, None]:
  40 |     async with AsyncSessionLocal() as session:
  41 |         try:
  42 |             yield session
  43 |         finally:
  44 |             await session.close()
  45 |

# Source code from: backend\app\core\kernel\models.py
-------------------------------------------------------
   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/kernel/models.py
   2 | # @file: Kernel Data Models (Kafka-Ready v2.1)
   3 | # @author: ansav8@gmail.com
   4 | # @description: Data Models for the Core Kernel.
   5 | # UPDATED: Added 'partition_key' and 'trace_id' for Distributed Relay.
   6 | 
   7 | from datetime import datetime
   8 | from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
   9 | 
  10 | from sqlalchemy import Integer, String, DateTime, Text
  11 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Mapped, mapped_column
  12 | from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB
  13 | 
  14 | from app.core.database.base import Base
  15 | 
  16 | class SystemOutbox(Base):
  17 |     """
  18 |     TRANSACTIONAL OUTBOX (The Kafka Waiting Room).
  19 |     Stores events atomically with business data.
  20 |     The 'Relay' process reads this table and pushes to Kafka.
  21 |     """
  22 |     __tablename__ = 'system_outbox'
  23 | 
  24 |     id: Mapped[int] = mapped_column(Integer, primary_key=True)
  25 |     
  26 |     # âš¡ KAFKA ROUTING
  27 |     # The Event Key (e.g. 'CONTAINER:GATE_IN')
  28 |     event_name: Mapped[str] = mapped_column(String(100), nullable=False)
  29 |     
  30 |     # Guaranteed Ordering Key (e.g. 'container_123', 'user_456')
  31 |     # All events for the same entity MUST have the same partition_key
  32 |     partition_key: Mapped[str] = mapped_column(String(100), nullable=False, index=True, default="global")
  33 |     
  34 |     # Distributed Trace ID (OpenTelemetry compatible)
  35 |     trace_id: Mapped[Optional[str]] = mapped_column(String(50), nullable=True)
  36 |     
  37 |     # The actual payload (Schema Versioned)
  38 |     payload: Mapped[Dict[str, Any]] = mapped_column(JSONB, nullable=False)
  39 |     
  40 |     # Metadata for legacy tracing
  41 |     entity_id: Mapped[Optional[int]] = mapped_column(Integer, nullable=True) 
  42 |     created_at: Mapped[datetime] = mapped_column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
  43 |     
  44 |     # âš¡ PROCESSING STATUS
  45 |     # PENDING   : Ready to be sent to Kafka
  46 |     # PUBLISHED : Successfully sent to Kafka (Acked)
  47 |     # FAILED    : Kafka rejected it (Poison Pill)
  48 |     status: Mapped[str] = mapped_column(String(20), default='PENDING', index=True) 
  49 |     
  50 |     processed_at: Mapped[Optional[datetime]] = mapped_column(DateTime, nullable=True)
  51 |     retry_count: Mapped[int] = mapped_column(Integer, default=0)
  52 |     error_log: Mapped[Optional[str]] = mapped_column(Text, nullable=True)
  53 | 
  54 |     def to_dict(self):
  55 |         """
  56 |         Serialization helper for the Relay.
  57 |         """
  58 |         return {
  59 |             'id': self.id,
  60 |             'event': self.event_name,
  61 |             'key': self.partition_key,
  62 |             'payload': self.payload,
  63 |             'trace_id': self.trace_id,
  64 |             'timestamp': self.created_at.isoformat() if self.created_at else None
  65 |         }

   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/meta/constants.py
   2 | # @file: Meta-Kernel Constants (The Vocabulary)
   3 | # @author: The Engineer (ansav8@gmail.com)
   4 | # @description: Defines the Immutable Truths for the Adaptive Data Engine.
   5 | # UPDATED: Injected ACTION_METADATA to enable "Dumb UI" rendering.
   6 | # @security-level: LEVEL 0 (Kernel)
   7 | 
   8 | from enum import Enum, unique
   9 | 
  10 | @unique
  11 | class BindingType(str, Enum):
  12 |     """The Jurisdiction Class. Defines WHAT we are binding to."""
  13 |     ENTITY = "ENTITY"       # A physical Database Table (e.g. USER, CONTAINER)
  14 |     GROUP = "GROUP"         # A virtual Tag or Job ID (e.g. NIGHTLY_SYNC, VIP_TIER)
  15 | 
  16 | @unique
  17 | class AttributeType(str, Enum):
  18 |     """The Data Type. Defines how the value is stored and validated."""
  19 |     TEXT = "TEXT"
  20 |     TEXTAREA = "TEXTAREA"
  21 |     RICH_TEXT = "RICH_TEXT"
  22 |     NUMBER = "NUMBER"
  23 |     BOOLEAN = "BOOLEAN"
  24 |     SELECT = "SELECT"
  25 |     MULTI_SELECT = "MULTI_SELECT"
  26 |     DATE = "DATE"
  27 |     DATETIME = "DATETIME"
  28 |     TIME = "TIME"
  29 |     REFERENCE = "REFERENCE"
  30 |     FILE = "FILE"
  31 |     JSON = "JSON"
  32 |     FORMULA = "FORMULA"
  33 | 
  34 | @unique
  35 | class WidgetType(str, Enum):
  36 |     """The Interface Hint. Defines how the field is rendered."""
  37 |     # Text
  38 |     INPUT = "INPUT"
  39 |     TEXTAREA = "TEXTAREA"
  40 |     RICH_TEXT = "RICH_TEXT"
  41 |     EMAIL = "EMAIL"
  42 |     PHONE = "PHONE"
  43 |     COLOR = "COLOR"
  44 |     
  45 |     # Numeric
  46 |     NUMBER = "NUMBER"
  47 |     SLIDER = "SLIDER"
  48 |     CURRENCY = "CURRENCY"
  49 |     PERCENTAGE = "PERCENTAGE"
  50 |     
  51 |     # Choice

# Source code from: backend\app\core\meta\engine.py
-----------------------------------------------------
   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/meta/engine.py
   2 | # @file Meta-Kernel Policy Engine (The Brain)
   3 | # @author The Engineer (ansav8@gmail.com)
   4 | # @description The Runtime Processor for Level 5 Policy Enforcement.
   5 | #              UPDATED: Added 'Value Resolution' for SET_VALUE and TRIGGER_EVENT.
   6 | #              This allows policies to use variables (e.g. actor.id) instead of just static strings.
   7 | 
   8 | import jmespath
   9 | import logging
  10 | from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
  11 | from datetime import datetime
  12 | 
  13 | from app.core.kernel.actions import LogicResult
  14 | from app.core.meta.models import PolicyDefinition
  15 | from app.core.meta.constants import PolicyResolutionStrategy, RuleActionType
  16 | 
  17 | logger = logging.getLogger("core.meta.engine")
  18 | 
  19 | class PolicyEngine:
  20 |     """
  21 |     The Universal Logic Executor.
  22 |     Input: Data + Policies
  23 |     Output: LogicResult (Pass/Fail + Messages)
  24 |     """
  25 | 
  26 |     def evaluate(
  27 |         self, 
  28 |         entity: Dict[str, Any], 
  29 |         policies: List[PolicyDefinition], 
  30 |         strategy: str = PolicyResolutionStrategy.ALL_MUST_PASS,
  31 |         context_override: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
  32 |     ) -> LogicResult:
  33 |         """
  34 |         The Main Entry Point.
  35 |         Evaluates a set of policies against an entity.
  36 |         """
  37 |         start_time = datetime.now()
  38 |         
  39 |         # 1. Prepare Data Context (Sandbox Envelope)
  40 |         # We wrap the data to allow 'context.meta' or 'context.actor' access if needed later.
  41 |         data_context = context_override or {}
  42 |         if not data_context:
  43 |             data_context = entity if isinstance(entity, dict) else self._serialize(entity)
  44 |         
  45 |         # Strategy: Pass object directly. Rules should be written as `host.weight > 10`.
  46 |         
  47 |         combined_result = LogicResult(is_valid=True)
  48 |         executed_count = 0
  49 |         violation_count = 0
  50 | 
  51 |         # 2. Iterate Policies
  52 |         for policy in policies:
  53 |             if not policy.is_active:
  54 |                 continue
  55 | 
  56 |             policy_result = self._evaluate_single_policy(policy, data_context)
  57 |             executed_count += 1
  58 | 
  59 |             # 3. Merge Results based on Governance Strategy
  60 |             if not policy_result.is_valid:
  61 |                 violation_count += 1
  62 |                 combined_result.blocking_errors.extend(policy_result.blocking_errors)
  63 |                 combined_result.is_valid = False # Temporarily mark false, Strategy decides final
  64 |             
  65 |             combined_result.warnings.extend(policy_result.warnings)
  66 |             combined_result.mutations.extend(policy_result.mutations)
  67 |             combined_result.side_effects.extend(policy_result.side_effects)
  68 | 
  69 |         # 4. Apply Resolution Strategy ( The Judge )
  70 |         final_verdict = self._apply_strategy(strategy, combined_result, executed_count, violation_count)
  71 |         
  72 |         duration = (datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds() * 1000
  73 |         self._log_summary(final_verdict, executed_count, duration)
  74 |         
  75 |         return final_verdict
  76 | 
  77 |     def _evaluate_single_policy(self, policy: PolicyDefinition, data: Any) -> LogicResult:
  78 |         """
  79 |         Executes one Policy Bundle (which may contain multiple Rules).
  80 |         """
  81 |         result = LogicResult(is_valid=True)
  82 |         
  83 |         # Policies store rules as a JSONB list: [{ "logic": "...", "action": "BLOCK", ... }]
  84 |         rules = policy.rules if isinstance(policy.rules, list) else []
  85 |         
  86 |         for rule in rules:
  87 |             try:
  88 |                 logic_expr = rule.get("logic", "")
  89 |                 action = rule.get("action", RuleActionType.BLOCK)
  90 |                 message = rule.get("message", f"Policy '{policy.key}' violation.")
  91 |                 
  92 |                 # A. Execute JMESPath
  93 |                 # Boolean expressions: `host.age > 18` returns True/False.
  94 |                 is_match = jmespath.search(logic_expr, data)
  95 |                 
  96 |                 # B. Handle Match (Triggered)
  97 |                 if is_match:
  98 |                     # âš¡ RESOLVE DYNAMIC VALUES
  99 |                     # If action involves data, we must check if the value is a reference (e.g. actor.id)
 100 |                     raw_value = rule.get("value")
 101 |                     resolved_value = self._resolve_value(raw_value, data)
 102 | 
 103 |                     if action == RuleActionType.BLOCK:
 104 |                         result.is_valid = False
 105 |                         result.blocking_errors.append(message)
 106 |                     
 107 |                     elif action == RuleActionType.WARN:
 108 |                         result.warnings.append(message)
 109 |                     
 110 |                     elif action == RuleActionType.SET_VALUE:
 111 |                         result.mutations.append({
 112 |                             "target": rule.get("target"),
 113 |                             "value": resolved_value # ðŸ‘ˆ NOW RESOLVED
 114 |                         })
 115 | 
 116 |                     elif action == RuleActionType.TRIGGER_EVENT:
 117 |                         result.side_effects.append({
 118 |                             "type": "TRIGGER_EVENT",
 119 |                             "value": {
 120 |                                 "event": rule.get("value", {}).get("event"),
 121 |                                 "payload": rule.get("value", {}).get("payload") # TODO: recursive resolve here if needed
 122 |                             }
 123 |                         })
 124 |                         
 125 |                     elif action == RuleActionType.TRANSITION:
 126 |                         result.side_effects.append({
 127 |                             "type": "TRANSITION",
 128 |                             "value": resolved_value
 129 |                         })
 130 | 
 131 |             except Exception as e:
 132 |                 # SAFEGUARD: Bad rule syntax should not crash the system.
 133 |                 logger.error(f"ðŸ”¥ [PolicyEngine] Rule Crash in '{policy.key}': {e}")
 134 |                 
 135 |                 # âš¡ FAIL OPEN: Treat crash as WARNING, not BLOCK.
 136 |                 result.warnings.append(f"System Governance Warning: Rule crashed in '{policy.key}'. Logic ignored.")
 137 |         
 138 |         return result
 139 | 
 140 |     def _resolve_value(self, value: Any, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> Any:
 141 |         """
 142 |         Detects if a value is a reference (e.g. 'actor.id') and resolves it against the context.
 143 |         """
 144 |         if not isinstance(value, str):
 145 |             return value
 146 |         
 147 |         # Heuristic: If it looks like a known context path, try to resolve it.
 148 |         # This matches the 'Value Source' logic in the Frontend Policy Editor.
 149 |         KNOWN_ROOTS = ['host.', 'meta.', 'system.', 'actor.', 'session.', 'context.']
 150 |         
 151 |         if any(value.startswith(root) for root in KNOWN_ROOTS):
 152 |             try:
 153 |                 resolved = jmespath.search(value, context)
 154 |                 # If resolution works, return it. If it returns None, it might mean the field is missing,
 155 |                 # but we return None rather than the string literal "actor.id".
 156 |                 return resolved
 157 |             except Exception:
 158 |                 # If JMESPath crashes, fallback to the string literal
 159 |                 return value
 160 |         
 161 |         return value
 162 | 
 163 |     def _apply_strategy(self, strategy: str, result: LogicResult, total: int, violations: int) -> LogicResult:
 164 |         """
 165 |         Decides the final outcome based on the strategy.
 166 |         """
 167 |         if total == 0:
 168 |             return result # No policies = Pass
 169 | 
 170 |         if strategy == PolicyResolutionStrategy.ALL_MUST_PASS:
 171 |             # Default: Any violation kills the transaction
 172 |             if violations > 0:
 173 |                 result.is_valid = False
 174 |             else:
 175 |                 result.is_valid = True
 176 | 
 177 |         elif strategy == PolicyResolutionStrategy.AT_LEAST_ONE:
 178 |             # If (Total - Violations) > 0, then Pass.
 179 |             if (total - violations) > 0:
 180 |                 result.is_valid = True
 181 |                 result.blocking_errors = [] # Clear errors if we passed via override
 182 |             else:
 183 |                 result.is_valid = False
 184 | 
 185 |         return result
 186 | 
 187 |     def _serialize(self, entity: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 188 |         """Helper to convert SQLAlchemy objects to Dict for JMESPath."""
 189 |         if hasattr(entity, "to_dict"):
 190 |             return entity.to_dict()
 191 |         if hasattr(entity, "__dict__"):
 192 |             return {c.name: getattr(entity, c.name) for c in entity.__table__.columns}
 193 |         return str(entity)
 194 | 
 195 |     def _log_summary(self, result: LogicResult, count: int, duration: float):
 196 |         if not result.is_valid:
 197 |             logger.info(f"ðŸš« [PolicyEngine] BLOCKED ({len(result.blocking_errors)} errors) | {count} Policies | {duration:.2f}ms")
 198 |         elif result.warnings:
 199 |             logger.info(f"âš ï¸ [PolicyEngine] WARNED ({len(result.warnings)} warnings) | {count} Policies | {duration:.2f}ms")
 200 |         else:
 201 |             logger.debug(f"âœ… [PolicyEngine] ALLOWED | {count} Policies | {duration:.2f}ms")
 202 | 
 203 | # Singleton
 204 | policy_engine = PolicyEngine()
 205 |

# Source code from: backend\app\core\meta\features\groups\service.py
----------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/meta/features/groups/service.py
   2 | # @file Policy Group Service
   3 | # @author The Engineer (ansav8@gmail.com)
   4 | # @description Business Logic for managing Policy Groups (Bundles).
   5 | #              Handles Creation, Member Management (Ordering), and Lifecycle.
   6 | 
   7 | import logging
   8 | from typing import List, Optional
   9 | from sqlalchemy import select, update, delete
  10 | from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
  11 | from sqlalchemy.orm import selectinload
  12 | 
  13 | from app.core.meta.models import PolicyGroup, PolicyDefinition
  14 | from app.core.meta.schemas import PolicyGroupCreate, PolicyGroupUpdate
  15 | 
  16 | logger = logging.getLogger("core.meta.groups")
  17 | 
  18 | class GroupService:
  19 |     """
  20 |     The Librarian. Manages collections of Policies.
  21 |     """
  22 | 
  23 |     @staticmethod
  24 |     def _generate_key(name: str) -> str:
  25 |         """Auto-generates a system key from a human name if not provided."""
  26 |         return name.upper().replace(" ", "_").replace("-", "_")
  27 | 
  28 |     @staticmethod
  29 |     async def create_group(db: AsyncSession, payload: PolicyGroupCreate) -> PolicyGroup:
  30 |         """
  31 |         Creates a new Policy Group.
  32 |         Enforces Key Uniqueness.
  33 |         """
  34 |         # 1. Validate Key Uniqueness
  35 |         stmt = select(PolicyGroup).where(PolicyGroup.key == payload.key)
  36 |         existing = await db.execute(stmt)
  37 |         if existing.scalars().first():
  38 |             raise ValueError(f"Group with key '{payload.key}' already exists.")
  39 | 
  40 |         # 2. Validate Policy Keys (Optional but recommended)
  41 |         # We trust the user provided valid keys, or we could verify them here.
  42 |         
  43 |         # 3. Create Entity
  44 |         db_obj = PolicyGroup(
  45 |             key=payload.key,
  46 |             name=payload.name,
  47 |             description=payload.description,
  48 |             policy_keys=payload.policy_keys, # Stores order: ["SECURITY_V1", "LOGGING_V2"]
  49 |             is_active=payload.is_active
  50 |         )
  51 |         
  52 |         db.add(db_obj)
  53 |         
  54 |         try:
  55 |             await db.commit()
  56 |             await db.refresh(db_obj)
  57 |             logger.info(f"ðŸ“¦ [GroupService] Created Bundle: {db_obj.key}")
  58 |             return db_obj
  59 |         except Exception as e:
  60 |             await db.rollback()
  61 |             logger.error(f"ðŸ”¥ [GroupService] Creation Failed: {e}")
  62 |             raise e
  63 | 
  64 |     @staticmethod
  65 |     async def get_groups(db: AsyncSession, active_only: bool = True) -> List[PolicyGroup]:
  66 |         """
  67 |         Lists all Policy Groups.
  68 |         """
  69 |         query = select(PolicyGroup)
  70 |         if active_only:
  71 |             query = query.where(PolicyGroup.is_active == True)
  72 |             
  73 |         query = query.order_by(PolicyGroup.key)
  74 |         
  75 |         result = await db.execute(query)
  76 |         return result.scalars().all()
  77 | 
  78 |     @staticmethod
  79 |     async def get_group_by_id(db: AsyncSession, group_id: int) -> Optional[PolicyGroup]:
  80 |         """
  81 |         Fetches a single group.
  82 |         """
  83 |         return await db.get(PolicyGroup, group_id)
  84 | 
  85 |     @staticmethod
  86 |     async def update_group(db: AsyncSession, group_id: int, payload: PolicyGroupUpdate) -> Optional[PolicyGroup]:
  87 |         """
  88 |         Updates metadata or membership order.
  89 |         """
  90 |         group = await db.get(PolicyGroup, group_id)
  91 |         if not group:
  92 |             return None
  93 | 
  94 |         # Apply Updates
  95 |         update_data = payload.model_dump(exclude_unset=True)
  96 |         for key, value in update_data.items():
  97 |             setattr(group, key, value)
  98 | 
  99 |         try:
 100 |             await db.commit()
 101 |             await db.refresh(group)
 102 |             logger.info(f"ðŸ“ [GroupService] Updated Group: {group.key}")
 103 |             return group
 104 |         except Exception as e:
 105 |             await db.rollback()
 106 |             raise e
 107 | 
 108 |     @staticmethod
 109 |     async def delete_group(db: AsyncSession, group_id: int) -> bool:
 110 |         """
 111 |         Soft Delete (Deactivate) or Hard Delete if no dependencies.
 112 |         For now, we enforce Soft Delete to protect history.
 113 |         """
 114 |         group = await db.get(PolicyGroup, group_id)
 115 |         if not group:
 116 |             return False
 117 | 
 118 |         # TODO: Check if bound to any active PolicyBinding before deleting?
 119 |         # For Level 5 safety, we just Deactivate.
 120 |         group.is_active = False
 121 |         
 122 |         try:
 123 |             await db.commit()
 124 |             logger.info(f"ðŸš« [GroupService] Deactivated Group: {group.key}")
 125 |             return True
 126 |         except Exception as e:
 127 |             await db.rollback()
 128 |             raise e
 129 |

# Source code from: backend\app\core\meta\features\states\models.py
---------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/meta/features/states/models.py
   2 | # @file: State Engine Data Models
   3 | # @author: The Engineer
   4 | # @description: Defines the 'Class' of a Workflow (e.g. WIZARD vs JOB).
   5 | # Replaces hardcoded Enums with Database Rows.
   6 | # @security-level: LEVEL 9 (Strict Schema)
   7 | 
   8 | from sqlalchemy import Column, String, DateTime, Text
   9 | from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB
  10 | from sqlalchemy.sql import func, text
  11 | 
  12 | from app.core.database.base import Base
  13 | 
  14 | class WorkflowType(Base):
  15 |     """
  16 |     Defines a Category of State Machine.
  17 |     
  18 |     Acts as a Template/Class for 'StateDefinition'.
  19 |     - key: 'WIZARD', 'JOB'
  20 |     - validation_schema: JSON Schema used to validate the 'transitions' blob.
  21 |     - ui_config: Frontend hints (default icon, color, label).
  22 |     """
  23 |     __tablename__ = "meta_workflow_types"
  24 | 
  25 |     # Identity
  26 |     key = Column(String(50), primary_key=True, index=True) # WIZARD, JOB, GOVERNANCE
  27 |     label = Column(String(100), nullable=False)            # "Interactive Wizard"
  28 |     description = Column(String(500), nullable=True)
  29 | 
  30 |     # âš¡ THE BRAIN: Dynamic Validation Logic
  31 |     # Instead of hardcoding "if type == WIZARD check form_schema",
  32 |     # we store the JSON Schema here and validate dynamically.
  33 |     validation_schema = Column(JSONB, nullable=False, server_default=text("'{}'::jsonb"))
  34 | 
  35 |     # âš¡ UI HINTS (Future Proofing)
  36 |     # e.g. { "icon": "ant:RocketOutlined", "color": "blue" }
  37 |     ui_config = Column(JSONB, nullable=False, server_default=text("'{}'::jsonb"))
  38 | 
  39 |     # Audit
  40 |     created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
  41 |     updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
  42 | 
  43 |     def __repr__(self):
  44 |         return f"<WorkflowType(key='{self.key}')>"

  13 | # --- VALIDATION LOGIC ---
  14 | def validate_xstate_structure(machine: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
  15 |     """Forensic audit of the State Machine JSON."""
  16 |     if "id" not in machine:
  17 |         raise ValueError("XState Machine must have an 'id'.")
  18 |     if "initial" not in machine:
  19 |         raise ValueError("XState Machine must have an 'initial' state.")
  20 |     if "states" not in machine or not isinstance(machine["states"], dict):
  21 |         raise ValueError("XState Machine must have a 'states' dictionary.")
  22 |     return machine
  23 |

   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/meta/features/states/service.py
   2 | # @file: State Engine Service
   3 | # @author: The Engineer
   4 | # @description: Manages Lifecycle Flows.
   5 | # @security-level: LEVEL 9 (Safety Interlocks)
   6 | # @updated: Restored 'get_workflow_types' and wired 'ScopeValidator.validate'.
   7 | 
   8 | import logging
   9 | from typing import List, Optional
  10 | from sqlalchemy import select, update, desc
  11 | from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
  12 | 
  13 | from app.core.meta.models import StateDefinition
  14 | from app.core.meta.features.states.models import WorkflowType # âš¡ RESTORED IMPORT
  15 | from app.domains.system.models import KernelScope 
  16 | from app.core.meta.features.states.schemas import StateMachineCreate
  17 | from app.core.meta.features.states.logic.validator import ScopeValidator
  18 | 
  19 | logger = logging.getLogger("core.meta.states")
  20 | 
  21 | class StateService:
  22 | 
  23 |     @staticmethod
  24 |     async def get_workflow_types(db: AsyncSession) -> List[WorkflowType]:
  25 |         """
  26 |         Retrieves the catalogue of available Workflow "Animals" (e.g. WIZARD, JOB).
  27 |         Used by the Frontend to dynamically render the "Create New" menu.
  28 |         """
  29 |         # Order by key for consistent UI rendering
  30 |         stmt = select(WorkflowType).order_by(WorkflowType.key)
  31 |         result = await db.execute(stmt)
  32 |         return result.scalars().all()
  33 | 
  34 |     @staticmethod
  35 |     async def create_machine(db: AsyncSession, payload: StateMachineCreate) -> StateDefinition:
  36 |         """
  37 |         Registers a State Machine (Ledger Strategy).
  38 |         1. Validate against Kernel Registry (Level 7) - NOW DYNAMIC.
  39 |         2. Archive Old Versions.
  40 |         3. Insert New Version (Auto-SemVer).
  41 |         """
  42 |         logger.info(f"ðŸ§¬ [StateEngine] Ratifying Process: {payload.domain}/{payload.scope}")
  43 | 
  44 |         try:
  45 |             # --- 0. LEVEL 7 INTEGRITY CHECK ---
  46 |             scope_stmt = select(KernelScope).where(
  47 |                 KernelScope.domain_key == payload.domain,
  48 |                 KernelScope.key == payload.scope
  49 |             )
  50 |             scope_result = await db.execute(scope_stmt)
  51 |             kernel_scope = scope_result.scalars().first()
  52 | 
  53 |             if not kernel_scope:
  54 |                 logger.warning(f"âš ï¸ [StateEngine] Scope '{payload.scope}' not found in Registry. Skipping strict validation.")
  55 |             else:
  56 |                 logger.info(f"âš–ï¸ [StateEngine] Validating against Scope Type: {kernel_scope.type}")
  57 |                 
  58 |                 # âš¡ UPDATE: Pass 'db' to allow dynamic rule lookup
  59 |                 await ScopeValidator.validate(db, payload.definition, kernel_scope.type)
  60 |                 
  61 |                 if kernel_scope.target_field and kernel_scope.target_field != payload.governed_field:
  62 |                     logger.warning(f"âš ï¸ [StateEngine] Payload target '{payload.governed_field}' differs from Registry '{kernel_scope.target_field}'.")
  63 | 
  64 |             # --- 1. Determine Next Version (SemVer + Legacy) ---
  65 |             # We fetch the absolute latest version to calculate the increment
  66 |             stmt = select(StateDefinition).where(
  67 |                 StateDefinition.entity_key == payload.domain,
  68 |                 StateDefinition.scope == payload.scope
  69 |             ).order_by(
  70 |                 desc(StateDefinition.version_major),
  71 |                 desc(StateDefinition.version_minor),
  72 |                 desc(StateDefinition.version_patch)
  73 |             ).limit(1)
  74 |             
  75 |             result = await db.execute(stmt)
  76 |             latest = result.scalars().first()
  77 |             
  78 |             if latest:
  79 |                 # Patch Increment Strategy (1.0.0 -> 1.0.1)
  80 |                 new_major = latest.version_major
  81 |                 new_minor = latest.version_minor
  82 |                 new_patch = latest.version_patch + 1
  83 |                 next_legacy_ver = (latest.version or 0) + 1
  84 |             else:
  85 |                 # Initialize at 1.0.0
  86 |                 new_major = 1
  87 |                 new_minor = 0
  88 |                 new_patch = 0
  89 |                 next_legacy_ver = 1
  90 | 
  91 |             # --- 2. Archive Old Versions ---
  92 |             if latest:
  93 |                 archive_stmt = update(StateDefinition).where(
  94 |                     StateDefinition.entity_key == payload.domain,
  95 |                     StateDefinition.scope == payload.scope,
  96 |                     StateDefinition.is_active == True
  97 |                 ).values(is_active=False)
  98 |                 await db.execute(archive_stmt)
  99 | 
 100 |             # --- 3. Create New Version ---
 101 |             db_obj = StateDefinition(
 102 |                 entity_key=payload.domain,
 103 |                 scope=payload.scope,
 104 |                 name=payload.name,
 105 |                 initial_state=payload.definition.get("initial"),
 106 |                 transitions=payload.definition, 
 107 |                 
 108 |                 # SemVer
 109 |                 version_major=new_major,
 110 |                 version_minor=new_minor,
 111 |                 version_patch=new_patch,
 112 |                 
 113 |                 # Legacy
 114 |                 version=next_legacy_ver,
 115 |                 
 116 |                 is_active=True,   
 117 |                 governed_field=payload.governed_field
 118 |             )
 119 |             
 120 |             db.add(db_obj)
 121 |             await db.commit()
 122 |             await db.refresh(db_obj)
 123 |             
 124 |             logger.info(f"âœ… [StateEngine] Ratified Version {new_major}.{new_minor}.{new_patch}: {payload.domain}/{payload.scope}")
 125 |             return db_obj
 126 | 
 127 |         except Exception as e:
 128 |             await db.rollback()
 129 |             logger.error(f"ðŸ”¥ [StateEngine] Ratification Failed: {str(e)}")
 130 |             raise e
 131 | 
 132 |     @staticmethod
 133 |     async def get_machines(db: AsyncSession, domain: Optional[str] = None) -> List[StateDefinition]:
 134 |         query = select(StateDefinition).where(StateDefinition.is_active == True)
 135 |         if domain:
 136 |             query = query.where(StateDefinition.entity_key == domain)
 137 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 138 |         return result.scalars().all()
 139 | 
 140 |     @staticmethod
 141 |     async def get_machine_by_scope(db: AsyncSession, domain: str, scope: str, version: Optional[int] = None) -> Optional[StateDefinition]:
 142 |         stmt = select(StateDefinition).where(
 143 |             StateDefinition.entity_key == domain,
 144 |             StateDefinition.scope == scope
 145 |         )
 146 |         if version:
 147 |             stmt = stmt.where(StateDefinition.version == version)
 148 |         else:
 149 |             stmt = stmt.where(StateDefinition.is_active == True)
 150 | 
 151 |         result = await db.execute(stmt)
 152 |         return result.scalars().first()
 153 | 
 154 |     @staticmethod
 155 |     async def get_machine_history(db: AsyncSession, domain: str, scope: str) -> List[StateDefinition]:
 156 |         stmt = select(StateDefinition).where(
 157 |             StateDefinition.entity_key == domain,
 158 |             StateDefinition.scope == scope
 159 |         ).order_by(
 160 |             desc(StateDefinition.version_major),
 161 |             desc(StateDefinition.version_minor),
 162 |             desc(StateDefinition.version_patch)
 163 |         )
 164 |         result = await db.execute(stmt)
 165 |         return result.scalars().all()
 166 | 
 167 |     @staticmethod
 168 |     async def delete_machine(db: AsyncSession, id: int) -> bool:
 169 |         """
 170 |         Safe Deletion Protocol.
 171 |         """
 172 |         workflow = await db.get(StateDefinition, id)
 173 |         if not workflow: 
 174 |             return False
 175 | 
 176 |         logger.info(f"ðŸ—‘ï¸ [StateEngine] Requesting deletion of {workflow.entity_key}/{workflow.scope}...")
 177 | 
 178 |         try:
 179 |             from app.domains.workspace.models import ActiveApp
 180 |             
 181 |             scope_stmt = select(KernelScope.id).where(
 182 |                 KernelScope.domain_key == workflow.entity_key,
 183 |                 KernelScope.key == workflow.scope
 184 |             )
 185 |             scope_id_res = await db.execute(scope_stmt)
 186 |             scope_id = scope_id_res.scalar()
 187 | 
 188 |             if scope_id:
 189 |                 usage_stmt = select(ActiveApp).where(
 190 |                     ActiveApp.scope_id == scope_id,
 191 |                     ActiveApp.is_active == True
 192 |                 )
 193 |                 usage_res = await db.execute(usage_stmt)
 194 |                 active_app = usage_res.scalars().first()
 195 | 
 196 |                 if active_app:
 197 |                     msg = f"â›” Blocked: Workflow is used by App #{active_app.id} on Screen #{active_app.screen_id}."
 198 |                     logger.warning(msg)
 199 |                     raise ValueError(msg)
 200 |             
 201 |         except ValueError as ve:
 202 |             raise ve
 203 |         except ImportError:
 204 |             pass
 205 |         except Exception as e:
 206 |             logger.error(f"ðŸ”¥ [StateEngine] Dependency Check Failed: {e}")
 207 |             raise ValueError("System Error during dependency check.")
 208 | 
 209 |         await db.delete(workflow)
 210 |         await db.commit()
 211 |         return True
 212 |

   8 | 
   9 | from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
  10 | from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
  11 | from sqlalchemy import select
  12 | from app.core.meta.features.topology.schemas import TopologyNode, TopologyNodeType

  20 | class TopologyService:
  21 |     """
  22 |     The Cartographer of the Database.
  23 |     Scans Domains, Entities, and Scopes to build a navigational graph.
  24 |     """
  25 | 
  26 |     @staticmethod
  27 |     async def get_domain_topology(db: AsyncSession, domain_key: str) -> List[TopologyNode]:
  28 |         """
  29 |         Generates the Concrete Children for a specific Domain.
  30 |         """
  31 |         nodes: List[TopologyNode] = []
  32 |         
  33 |         try:
  34 |             # âš¡ 0A. FETCH DYNAMIC WORKFLOW TYPES (Async)
  35 |             stmt_types = select(WorkflowType)
  36 |             result_types = await db.execute(stmt_types)
  37 |             workflow_types = result_types.scalars().all()
  38 |             
  39 |             # âš¡ 0B. FETCH DOMAIN METADATA (Async)
  40 |             stmt_domain = select(KernelDomain).where(KernelDomain.key == domain_key)
  41 |             result_domain = await db.execute(stmt_domain)
  42 |             domain = result_domain.scalars().first()
  43 |             
  44 |             if not domain:
  45 |                 return []
  46 | 
  47 |             # âš¡ SAFETY: Resolve attributes defensively
  48 |             d_type = getattr(domain, 'domain_type', getattr(domain, 'type', 'STANDARD'))
  49 |             
  50 |             # ---------------------------------------------------------
  51 |             # 1. âš¡ ENTITY NODE (Data Dictionary)
  52 |             # ---------------------------------------------------------
  53 |             if d_type in ['STANDARD', 'SYSTEM', 'AUTH']: 
  54 |                 entity_icon = "antd:DatabaseOutlined"
  55 |                 
  56 |                 nodes.append(TopologyNode(
  57 |                     key=f"entity_{domain_key}",
  58 |                     label="Data Dictionary",
  59 |                     type=TopologyNodeType.ENTITY,
  60 |                     route=f"/dictionary/{domain_key}?domain={domain_key}",
  61 |                     icon=entity_icon,
  62 |                     description="Primary Relational Data Storage",
  63 |                     metadata={
  64 |                         "count": 1, 
  65 |                         "technical_key": domain_key,
  66 |                         "physical_target": domain_key.lower() + "s"
  67 |                     }
  68 |                 ))
  69 | 
  70 |             # ---------------------------------------------------------
  71 |             # 2. âš¡ GOVERNANCE NODE (Policies)
  72 |             # ---------------------------------------------------------
  73 |             nodes.append(TopologyNode(
  74 |                 key=f"gov_{domain_key}",
  75 |                 label="Governance Policy", 
  76 |                 type=TopologyNodeType.GOVERNANCE,
  77 |                 route=f"/governance/{domain_key}?domain={domain_key}",
  78 |                 icon="antd:SafetyCertificateOutlined",
  79 |                 description="State machine controlling entity lifecycle status.",
  80 |                 metadata={
  81 |                     "count": 2,
  82 |                     "technical_key": domain_key
  83 |                 }
  84 |             ))
  85 | 
  86 |             # ---------------------------------------------------------
  87 |             # 3. âš¡ WORKFLOW NODES (Scopes)
  88 |             # ---------------------------------------------------------
  89 |             stmt_scopes = select(KernelScope).where(KernelScope.domain_key == domain_key)
  90 |             result_scopes = await db.execute(stmt_scopes)
  91 |             scopes = result_scopes.scalars().all()
  92 | 
  93 |             if scopes:
  94 |                 for scope in scopes:
  95 |                     # âš¡ FETCH TYPE DEFINITION
  96 |                     workflow_type = next((wt for wt in workflow_types if wt.key == scope.type), None)
  97 |                     
  98 |                     # âš¡ DEFAULT ICONS
  99 |                     item_icon = workflow_type.ui_config.get('icon') if workflow_type else "antd:AppstoreOutlined"
 100 | 
 101 |                     # ---------------------------------------------------------
 102 |                     # âš¡ GROUPING LOGIC (The "Hierarchy Builder")
 103 |                     # ---------------------------------------------------------
 104 |                     
 105 |                     # Initialize vars
 106 |                     section_key = None
 107 |                     section_label = None
 108 |                     section_icon = None
 109 |                     subsection_key = None
 110 |                     subsection_label = None
 111 |                     subsection_icon = None
 112 | 
 113 |                     # CASE A: WORKFLOWS (Wizards, Jobs, Views, Governance Flows)
 114 |                     # We group these under "WORKFLOWS" -> "TYPE"
 115 |                     if scope.type in ['WIZARD', 'JOB', 'VIEW', 'GOVERNANCE']:
 116 |                         # Parent Folder
 117 |                         section_key = "WORKFLOWS"
 118 |                         section_label = "Workflows"
 119 |                         section_icon = "antd:PartitionOutlined"
 120 |                         
 121 |                         # Child Folder (The Sub-Tree)
 122 |                         # Use the Label from the Workflow Type Definition (e.g. "Interactive Wizard")
 123 |                         if workflow_type:
 124 |                             subsection_key = workflow_type.key
 125 |                             subsection_label = workflow_type.label
 126 |                             subsection_icon = workflow_type.ui_config.get('icon')
 127 |                         else:
 128 |                             # Fallback if type def missing
 129 |                             subsection_key = scope.type
 130 |                             subsection_label = scope.type.title()
 131 |                             subsection_icon = "antd:FolderOutlined"
 132 | 
 133 |                     # CASE B: FALLBACK
 134 |                     else:
 135 |                         section_key = workflow_type.key if workflow_type else scope.type
 136 |                         section_label = workflow_type.label if workflow_type else scope.type
 137 |                         section_icon = workflow_type.ui_config.get('icon') if workflow_type else "antd:FolderOutlined"
 138 |                     # ---------------------------------------------------------
 139 | 
 140 |                     nodes.append(TopologyNode(
 141 |                         key=f"scope_{scope.key}",
 142 |                         label=scope.label,
 143 |                         type=TopologyNodeType.SCOPE,
 144 |                         route=f"/app/{domain_key.lower()}-{scope.key.lower()}",
 145 |                         icon=item_icon,
 146 |                         description=workflow_type.description if workflow_type else "System Process",
 147 |                         metadata={
 148 |                             "scope_type": scope.type,
 149 |                             "target_entity": scope.target_field,
 150 |                             "technical_key": scope.key,
 151 |                             
 152 |                             # âš¡ HIERARCHY METADATA
 153 |                             "section_key": section_key,
 154 |                             "section_label": section_label,
 155 |                             "section_icon": section_icon,
 156 |                             "subsection_key": subsection_key,
 157 |                             "subsection_label": subsection_label,
 158 |                             "subsection_icon": subsection_icon
 159 |                         }
 160 |                     ))
 161 | 
 162 |             # ---------------------------------------------------------
 163 |             # 4. âš¡ CHILD DOMAINS (Sub-Modules)
 164 |             # ---------------------------------------------------------
 165 |             stmt_children = select(KernelDomain).where(KernelDomain.parent_domain == domain_key)
 166 |             result_children = await db.execute(stmt_children)
 167 |             children = result_children.scalars().all()
 168 |             
 169 |             for child in children:
 170 |                 c_icon = getattr(child, 'module_icon', getattr(child, 'icon', 'antd:FolderOutlined'))
 171 |                 if not c_icon: c_icon = 'antd:FolderOutlined'
 172 |                 
 173 |                 nodes.append(TopologyNode(
 174 |                     key=f"domain_{child.key}",
 175 |                     label=child.label,
 176 |                     type=TopologyNodeType.FOLDER,
 177 |                     route=f"/topology/{child.key}",
 178 |                     icon=c_icon,
 179 |                     description=child.module_label, 
 180 |                     metadata={
 181 |                         "is_domain": True,
 182 |                         "domain_key": child.key,
 183 |                         "technical_key": child.key,
 184 |                         "section_key": "CHILD_DOMAINS",
 185 |                         "section_label": "Sub-Modules",
 186 |                         "section_icon": "antd:FolderOpenOutlined"
 187 |                     }
 188 |                 ))
 189 | 
 190 |             return nodes
 191 |             
 192 |         except Exception as e:
 193 |             try:
 194 |                 attrs = dir(domain) if domain else "None"
 195 |                 logger.error(f"ðŸ”¥ [Topology] CRASH DETAILS. Valid Attributes on KernelDomain: {attrs}")
 196 |             except:
 197 |                 pass
 198 |             logger.error(f"ðŸ”¥ [Topology] CRASH processing domain '{domain_key}': {str(e)}")
 199 |             raise e

  13 | 
  14 | class WidgetDefinition(Base):
  15 |     """
  16 |     The 'App Store' entry for a UI Component.
  17 |     """
  18 |     __tablename__ = "meta_widget_definitions"
  19 | 
  20 |     id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)
  21 |     
  22 |     # IDENTITY
  23 |     key = Column(String(100), nullable=False, index=True) # e.g., "SECURE_PASSWORD"
  24 |     name = Column(String(255), nullable=False)            # e.g., "Secure Password Input"
  25 |     description = Column(String(500), nullable=True)
  26 |     
  27 |     # CLASSIFICATION
  28 |     category = Column(String(50), default="INPUT", index=True) # INPUT, DISPLAY, CONTAINER
  29 |     icon = Column(String(50), nullable=True) # e.g., "antd:LockOutlined"
  30 |     
  31 |     # THE CONTRACT (JSON Schema)
  32 |     # Defines what 'config' props are valid for this widget.
  33 |     props_schema = Column(JSONB, nullable=False, server_default=text("'{}'::jsonb"))
  34 |     
  35 |     # THE SIGNALS
  36 |     # Defines what events this widget can emit (e.g. ["CHANGE", "BLUR", "GENERATE"])
  37 |     events = Column(JSONB, nullable=False, server_default=text("'[]'::jsonb"))
  38 | 
  39 |     # SEMVER (Ledger Strategy)
  40 |     version_major = Column(Integer, default=1, nullable=False)
  41 |     version_minor = Column(Integer, default=0, nullable=False)
  42 |     version_patch = Column(Integer, default=0, nullable=False)
  43 |     
  44 |     is_latest = Column(Boolean, default=True, index=True)
  45 |     is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
  46 |     
  47 |     created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
  48 |     updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
  49 | 
  50 |     __table_args__ = (
  51 |         UniqueConstraint('key', 'version_major', 'version_minor', 'version_patch', name='uq_widget_key_version'),
  52 |     )
  53 | 
  54 |     @property
  55 |     def version(self) -> str:
  56 |         return f"{self.version_major}.{self.version_minor}.{self.version_patch}"
  57 | 
  58 |     def __repr__(self):
  59 |         return f"<WidgetDef(key='{self.key}', v={self.version})>"

  43 |     @staticmethod
  44 |     def validate_rule_syntax(rules: List[Dict[str, Any]]):
  45 |         for i, rule in enumerate(rules):
  46 |             logic = rule.get("logic", "")
  47 |             if not logic: continue 
  48 |             try:
  49 |                 jmespath.compile(logic)
  50 |             except Exception as e:
  51 |                 raise ValueError(f"Rule #{i+1} has invalid syntax: {logic}. Error: {str(e)}")

  54 |     #  1. POLICY DEFINITIONS
  55 |     # ==============================================================================
  56 | 
  57 |     @staticmethod
  58 |     async def create_policy(db: AsyncSession, payload: PolicyCreate) -> PolicyDefinition:
  59 |         query = select(PolicyDefinition).where(
  60 |             PolicyDefinition.key == payload.key,
  61 |             PolicyDefinition.is_latest == True
  62 |         )
  63 |         result = await db.execute(query)
  64 |         if result.scalars().first():
  65 |             raise ValueError(f"Policy with key '{payload.key}' already exists.")
  66 | 
  67 |         rules_data = [r.model_dump(mode='json') for r in payload.rules]
  68 |         MetaService.validate_rule_syntax(rules_data)
  69 | 
  70 |         db_obj = PolicyDefinition(
  71 |             key=payload.key,
  72 |             name=payload.name,
  73 |             description=payload.description,
  74 |             resolution=payload.resolution,
  75 |             rules=rules_data,
  76 |             tags=payload.tags, 
  77 |             is_active=payload.is_active,
  78 |             version_major=1,
  79 |             version_minor=0,
  80 |             is_latest=True
  81 |         )
  82 |         db.add(db_obj)
  83 |         await db.commit()
  84 |         await db.refresh(db_obj)
  85 |         return db_obj
  86 | 
  87 |     @staticmethod
  88 |     async def update_policy(db: AsyncSession, id: int, payload: PolicyUpdate) -> Optional[PolicyDefinition]:
  89 |         parent_policy = await db.get(PolicyDefinition, id)
  90 |         if not parent_policy: return None
  91 | 
  92 |         new_major = parent_policy.version_major
  93 |         new_minor = parent_policy.version_minor + 1
  94 |         
  95 |         if new_minor >= 100:
  96 |             new_major += 1
  97 |             new_minor = 0
  98 | 
  99 |         update_data = payload.model_dump(exclude_unset=True, mode='json')
 100 |         if "rules" in update_data:
 101 |             MetaService.validate_rule_syntax(update_data["rules"])
 102 | 
 103 |         new_policy = PolicyDefinition(
 104 |             key=parent_policy.key,
 105 |             name=update_data.get("name", parent_policy.name),
 106 |             description=update_data.get("description", parent_policy.description),
 107 |             resolution=update_data.get("resolution", parent_policy.resolution),
 108 |             rules=update_data.get("rules", parent_policy.rules),
 109 |             tags=update_data.get("tags", parent_policy.tags),
 110 |             is_active=update_data.get("is_active", parent_policy.is_active),
 111 |             version_major=new_major,
 112 |             version_minor=new_minor,
 113 |             is_latest=True
 114 |         )
 115 | 
 116 |         try:
 117 |             db.add(new_policy)
 118 |             await db.flush() 
 119 | 
 120 |             parent_policy.is_latest = False
 121 | 
 122 |             stmt_promote = update(PolicyBinding).\
 123 |                 where(PolicyBinding.policy_id == parent_policy.id).\
 124 |                 values(policy_id=new_policy.id)
 125 |             
 126 |             await db.execute(stmt_promote)
 127 |             
 128 |             await db.commit()
 129 |             await db.refresh(new_policy)
 130 |             await MetaService.invalidate_cache("ALL") 
 131 |             return new_policy
 132 |         except Exception as e:
 133 |             await db.rollback()
 134 |             raise e

 136 |     @staticmethod
 137 |     def dry_run_policy(policy_data: Dict[str, Any], context: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 138 |         temp_policy = PolicyDefinition(
 139 |             key="dry_run_temp",
 140 |             rules=policy_data.get("rules", []),
 141 |             is_active=True
 142 |         )
 143 |         result = policy_engine.evaluate(entity={}, policies=[temp_policy], context_override=context)
 144 |         return {
 145 |             "is_valid": result.is_valid,
 146 |             "blocking_errors": result.blocking_errors,
 147 |             "warnings": result.warnings,
 148 |             "mutations": result.mutations,
 149 |             "side_effects": result.side_effects
 150 |         }

 153 |     async def get_policy_history(db: AsyncSession, key: str) -> List[PolicyDefinition]:
 154 |         stmt = select(PolicyDefinition).where(
 155 |             PolicyDefinition.key == key
 156 |         ).order_by(
 157 |             desc(PolicyDefinition.version_major), 
 158 |             desc(PolicyDefinition.version_minor)
 159 |         )
 160 |         result = await db.execute(stmt)
 161 |         return result.scalars().all()

 163 |     @staticmethod
 164 |     async def restore_policy(db: AsyncSession, version_id: int) -> Optional[PolicyDefinition]:
 165 |         target_version = await db.get(PolicyDefinition, version_id)
 166 |         if not target_version: return None
 167 | 
 168 |         stmt_head = select(PolicyDefinition).where(
 169 |             PolicyDefinition.key == target_version.key,
 170 |             PolicyDefinition.is_latest == True
 171 |         )
 172 |         result = await db.execute(stmt_head)
 173 |         current_head = result.scalars().first()
 174 | 
 175 |         if not current_head:
 176 |             raise ValueError("Corrupt Timeline: No active head found for this policy.")
 177 | 
 178 |         restore_payload = PolicyUpdate(
 179 |             name=target_version.name,
 180 |             description=f"Restored from v{target_version.version_major}.{target_version.version_minor:02d}. {target_version.description}",
 181 |             resolution=target_version.resolution,
 182 |             rules=target_version.rules, 
 183 |             tags=target_version.tags,
 184 |             is_active=True
 185 |         )
 186 | 
 187 |         return await MetaService.update_policy(db, current_head.id, restore_payload)

 189 |     @staticmethod
 190 |     async def get_policies(db: AsyncSession, domain: Optional[str] = None) -> List[PolicyDefinition]:
 191 |         """
 192 |         âš¡ TAG-DRIVEN ARCHITECTURE: Filters policies by their domain tag.
 193 |         """
 194 |         query = select(PolicyDefinition).where(PolicyDefinition.is_latest == True)
 195 |         
 196 |         if domain and domain != "ALL":
 197 |             # JSONB contains check: tags @> '["domain:XYZ"]'
 198 |             query = query.where(PolicyDefinition.tags.contains([f"domain:{domain}"]))
 199 |             
 200 |         query = query.order_by(PolicyDefinition.key)
 201 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 202 |         return result.scalars().all()

 208 |     @staticmethod
 209 |     async def create_binding(db: AsyncSession, payload: PolicyBindingCreate) -> PolicyBinding:
 210 |         if payload.policy_id:
 211 |             policy = await db.get(PolicyDefinition, payload.policy_id)
 212 |             if not policy: raise ValueError("Policy ID not found.")
 213 |         
 214 |         if payload.policy_group_id:
 215 |              group = await db.get(PolicyGroup, payload.policy_group_id)
 216 |              if not group: raise ValueError("Group ID not found.")
 217 | 
 218 |         binding_data = payload.model_dump(mode='json')
 219 |         db_obj = PolicyBinding(**binding_data)
 220 |         db.add(db_obj)
 221 |         try:
 222 |             await db.commit()
 223 |             
 224 |             stmt = select(PolicyBinding)\
 225 |                 .options(selectinload(PolicyBinding.policy))\
 226 |                 .options(selectinload(PolicyBinding.group))\
 227 |                 .where(PolicyBinding.id == db_obj.id)
 228 |                 
 229 |             result = await db.execute(stmt)
 230 |             loaded_obj = result.scalars().first()
 231 |             
 232 |             await MetaService.invalidate_cache(payload.target_domain)
 233 |             
 234 |             # âš¡ KERNEL RELAY EMISSION
 235 |             event = SystemOutbox(
 236 |                 event_type="SWITCHBOARD:BINDING_CREATED",
 237 |                 entity_id=str(loaded_obj.id),
 238 |                 domain="META",
 239 |                 payload={"target_domain": loaded_obj.target_domain, "target_scope": loaded_obj.target_scope}
 240 |             )
 241 |             db.add(event)
 242 |             await db.commit()
 243 |             
 244 |             return loaded_obj
 245 | 
 246 |         except Exception as e:
 247 |             await db.rollback()
 248 |             raise e

 250 |     @staticmethod
 251 |     async def update_binding(db: AsyncSession, binding_id: int, payload: PolicyBindingUpdate) -> Optional[PolicyBinding]:
 252 |         query = select(PolicyBinding).where(PolicyBinding.id == binding_id)
 253 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 254 |         db_obj = result.scalars().first()
 255 |         if not db_obj: return None
 256 | 
 257 |         update_data = payload.model_dump(exclude_unset=True, mode='json')
 258 |         for field, value in update_data.items(): setattr(db_obj, field, value)
 259 |         await db.commit()
 260 |         
 261 |         query = select(PolicyBinding)\
 262 |             .options(selectinload(PolicyBinding.policy))\
 263 |             .options(selectinload(PolicyBinding.group))\
 264 |             .where(PolicyBinding.id == binding_id)
 265 |             
 266 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 267 |         loaded_obj = result.scalars().first()
 268 |         
 269 |         await MetaService.invalidate_cache(db_obj.target_domain)
 270 |         
 271 |         # âš¡ KERNEL RELAY EMISSION
 272 |         event = SystemOutbox(
 273 |             event_type="SWITCHBOARD:BINDING_UPDATED",
 274 |             entity_id=str(loaded_obj.id),
 275 |             domain="META",
 276 |             payload={"target_domain": loaded_obj.target_domain, "is_active": loaded_obj.is_active}
 277 |         )
 278 |         db.add(event)
 279 |         await db.commit()
 280 | 
 281 |         return loaded_obj

 283 |     @staticmethod
 284 |     async def delete_binding(db: AsyncSession, binding_id: int) -> Optional[str]:
 285 |         query = select(PolicyBinding).where(PolicyBinding.id == binding_id)
 286 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 287 |         db_obj = result.scalars().first()
 288 |         if not db_obj: return None
 289 | 
 290 |         status_action = ""
 291 |         target_domain = db_obj.target_domain
 292 | 
 293 |         if db_obj.is_active:
 294 |             db_obj.is_active = False
 295 |             status_action = "DEACTIVATED"
 296 |         else:
 297 |             await db.delete(db_obj)
 298 |             status_action = "DELETED"
 299 |         
 300 |         await db.commit()
 301 |         await MetaService.invalidate_cache(target_domain)
 302 |         
 303 |         # âš¡ KERNEL RELAY EMISSION
 304 |         event = SystemOutbox(
 305 |             event_type="SWITCHBOARD:BINDING_DELETED",
 306 |             entity_id=str(binding_id),
 307 |             domain="META",
 308 |             payload={"action": status_action, "target_domain": target_domain}
 309 |         )
 310 |         db.add(event)
 311 |         await db.commit()
 312 | 
 313 |         return status_action

 315 |     @staticmethod
 316 |     async def get_bindings(db: AsyncSession, domain: Optional[str] = None, scope: Optional[str] = None, search: Optional[str] = None) -> List[PolicyBinding]:
 317 |         stmt = select(PolicyBinding)\
 318 |             .options(selectinload(PolicyBinding.policy))\
 319 |             .options(selectinload(PolicyBinding.group))
 320 |         
 321 |         if domain and domain != "ALL": 
 322 |             stmt = stmt.where(PolicyBinding.target_domain == domain)
 323 |         if scope and scope != "ALL": 
 324 |             stmt = stmt.where(PolicyBinding.target_scope == scope)
 325 |             
 326 |         if search:
 327 |             stmt = stmt.join(PolicyDefinition, isouter=True) 
 328 |             stmt = stmt.where(PolicyDefinition.name.ilike(f"%{search}%"))
 329 |             
 330 |         result = await db.execute(stmt.order_by(desc(PolicyBinding.priority)))
 331 |         return result.scalars().all()

 333 |     @staticmethod
 334 |     async def get_switchboard_manifest(db: AsyncSession, domain: Optional[str] = None, search: Optional[str] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 335 |         """
 336 |         âš¡ THE DUMB UI FUSION ENGINE
 337 |         Reads all bindings and returns a completely formatted, view-ready dictionary
 338 |         so the frontend requires zero logic.
 339 |         """
 340 |         bindings = await MetaService.get_bindings(db, domain=domain, search=search)
 341 |         
 342 |         columns = [
 343 |             {"key": "source", "label": "Policy / Bundle Source", "data_type": "SOURCE_TAG"},
 344 |             {"key": "target", "label": "Jurisdiction Scope", "data_type": "SCOPE_TAG"},
 345 |             {"key": "status", "label": "Enforcement Status", "data_type": "STATUS"},
 346 |             {"key": "priority", "label": "Priority", "data_type": "PRIORITY_TAG"}
 347 |         ]
 348 |         
 349 |         actions = [
 350 |             {"key": "TOGGLE_ACTIVE", "label": "Toggle", "icon": "antd:SwapOutlined", "danger": False, "requires_confirmation": True, "confirmation_text": "Change enforcement status?"},
 351 |             {"key": "DELETE_BINDING", "label": "Remove", "icon": "antd:DeleteOutlined", "danger": True, "requires_confirmation": True, "confirmation_text": "Permanently remove this jurisdiction?"}
 352 |         ]
 353 | 
 354 |         data = []
 355 |         for b in bindings:
 356 |             # God Logic: Resolve Source
 357 |             if b.policy:
 358 |                 src_label = b.policy.name
 359 |                 src_type = "POLICY"
 360 |                 src_version = f"v{b.policy.version_major}.{b.policy.version_minor}"
 361 |                 src_icon = "antd:FileProtectOutlined"
 362 |                 src_color = "blue"
 363 |             elif b.group:
 364 |                 src_label = b.group.name
 365 |                 src_type = "BUNDLE"
 366 |                 src_version = f"({len(b.group.policy_keys)} rules)"
 367 |                 src_icon = "antd:AppstoreOutlined"
 368 |                 src_color = "cyan"
 369 |             else:
 370 |                 src_label = "Unknown"
 371 |                 src_type = "UNKNOWN"
 372 |                 src_version = ""
 373 |                 src_icon = "antd:QuestionOutlined"
 374 |                 src_color = "default"
 375 | 
 376 |             # God Logic: Resolve Target Icon
 377 |             target_icon = "antd:AppstoreOutlined"
 378 |             if b.target_scope == 'GLOBAL': target_icon = "antd:GlobalOutlined"
 379 |             elif b.target_scope == 'JOB': target_icon = "antd:RobotOutlined"
 380 |             elif b.target_scope == 'TRANSITION': target_icon = "antd:FieldTimeOutlined"
 381 |             elif b.target_scope == 'PROCESS': target_icon = "antd:ThunderboltOutlined"
 382 | 
 383 |             data.append({
 384 |                 "id": b.id,
 385 |                 "domain": b.target_domain,
 386 |                 "source": {
 387 |                     "label": src_label,
 388 |                     "type": src_type,
 389 |                     "version": src_version,
 390 |                     "icon": src_icon,
 391 |                     "color": src_color
 392 |                 },
 393 |                 "target": {
 394 |                     "scope": b.target_scope,
 395 |                     "context": b.target_context,
 396 |                     "icon": target_icon
 397 |                 },
 398 |                 "status": "ACTIVE" if b.is_active else "INACTIVE",
 399 |                 "priority": b.priority,
 400 |                 "is_active": b.is_active
 401 |             })
 402 |             
 403 |         return {
 404 |             "columns": columns,
 405 |             "actions": actions,
 406 |             "data": data
 407 |         }

 409 |     # ==============================================================================
 410 |     #  3. ATTRIBUTES (DICTIONARY)
 411 |     # ==============================================================================
 412 |     
 413 |     @staticmethod
 414 |     async def create_attribute(db: AsyncSession, payload: AttributeCreate) -> AttributeDefinition:
 415 |         domain_query = select(KernelDomain).options(selectinload(KernelDomain.type_def)).where(KernelDomain.key == payload.domain)
 416 |         domain_result = await db.execute(domain_query)
 417 |         domain_obj = domain_result.scalars().first()
 418 | 
 419 |         if domain_obj:
 420 |             props = domain_obj.type_def.properties if domain_obj.type_def and domain_obj.type_def.properties else {}
 421 |             if not props.get("supports_meta", True): 
 422 |                  logger.warning(f"â›” [Meta] Blocked attribute creation on locked domain: {payload.domain}")
 423 |                  raise ValueError(f"Domain '{payload.domain}' ({domain_obj.type_key}) is LOCKED. Custom attributes are forbidden.")
 424 | 
 425 |         query = select(AttributeDefinition).where(AttributeDefinition.domain == payload.domain, AttributeDefinition.key == payload.key)
 426 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 427 |         if result.scalars().first(): raise ValueError(f"Attribute '{payload.key}' already exists.")
 428 |         
 429 |         db_obj = AttributeDefinition(**payload.model_dump(mode='json'))
 430 |         db.add(db_obj)
 431 |         await db.commit()
 432 |         await db.refresh(db_obj)
 433 |         await MetaService.invalidate_cache(payload.domain)
 434 |         return db_obj
 435 | 
 436 |     @staticmethod
 437 |     async def get_attributes(db: AsyncSession, domain: str, active_only: bool = False) -> List[AttributeDefinition]:
 438 |         query = select(AttributeDefinition).where(AttributeDefinition.domain == domain)
 439 |         if active_only: query = query.where(AttributeDefinition.is_active == True)
 440 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 441 |         return result.scalars().all()
 442 | 
 443 |     @staticmethod
 444 |     async def update_attribute(db: AsyncSession, id: int, payload: AttributeUpdate) -> Optional[AttributeDefinition]:
 445 |         query = select(AttributeDefinition).where(AttributeDefinition.id == id)
 446 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 447 |         db_obj = result.scalars().first()
 448 |         if not db_obj: return None
 449 | 
 450 |         update_data = payload.model_dump(exclude_unset=True, mode='json')
 451 |         for field, value in update_data.items(): setattr(db_obj, field, value)
 452 |         await db.commit()
 453 |         await db.refresh(db_obj)
 454 |         await MetaService.invalidate_cache(db_obj.domain)
 455 |         return db_obj
 456 | 
 457 |     @staticmethod
 458 |     async def delete_attribute(db: AsyncSession, id: int) -> bool:
 459 |         query = select(AttributeDefinition).where(AttributeDefinition.id == id)
 460 |         result = await db.execute(query)
 461 |         db_obj = result.scalars().first()
 462 |         if not db_obj: return False
 463 | 
 464 |         if db_obj.is_system: raise ValueError("â›” System Attributes cannot be deleted.")
 465 |         await db.delete(db_obj)
 466 |         await db.commit()
 467 |         await MetaService.invalidate_cache(db_obj.domain)
 468 |         return True
 469 | 
 470 |     # ==============================================================================
 471 |     #  4. RULES (SIMPLE)
 472 |     # ==============================================================================
 473 | 
 474 |     @staticmethod
 475 |     async def create_rule(db: AsyncSession, payload: RuleCreate) -> RuleDefinition:
 476 |         db_obj = RuleDefinition(**payload.model_dump(mode='json'))
 477 |         db.add(db_obj)
 478 |         await db.commit()
 479 |         return db_obj
 480 | 
 481 |     @staticmethod
 482 |     async def get_rules(db: AsyncSession, domain: str, event_type: Optional[str] = None, scope: Optional[str] = None) -> List[RuleDefinition]:
 483 |         query = select(RuleDefinition).where(RuleDefinition.target_domain == domain, RuleDefinition.is_active == True)
 484 |         if event_type: query = query.where(RuleDefinition.event_type == event_type)
 485 |         if scope: query = query.where(or_(RuleDefinition.scope == scope, RuleDefinition.scope == None))
 486 |         result = await db.execute(query.order_by(desc(RuleDefinition.priority)))
 487 |         return result.scalars().all()
 488 | 
 489 |     # ==============================================================================
 490 |     #  5. SYSTEM & REFLECTION (THE FIX)
 491 |     # ==============================================================================
 492 | 
 493 |     @staticmethod
 494 |     async def get_fused_schema(db: AsyncSession, domain: str, active_only: bool = True) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 495 |         """
 496 |         The Brain: Combines Immutable Code (Registry) with Flexible Data (DB).
 497 |         Returns a Frontend-Ready Schema Object.
 498 |         """
 499 |         try:
 500 |             # âš¡ LOGGING: Trace the Fusion Step
 501 |             logger.info(f"ðŸ§© [Schema] Fusing domain: {domain}")
 502 | 
 503 |             fields = {}
 504 | 
 505 |             # 1. FETCH STATIC SCHEMA (The Bedrock)
 506 |             logger.debug(f"   â†³ [Schema] Fetching Static Registry for {domain}...")
 507 |             static_schema = domain_registry.get_schema(domain)
 508 |             
 509 |             if static_schema:
 510 |                 for key, def_ in static_schema.items():
 511 |                     fields[key] = {
 512 |                         "id": 0, # Static fields don't have a DB ID
 513 |                         "key": key,
 514 |                         "label": def_.get("label", key),
 515 |                         "description": def_.get("description", "System Field"),
 516 |                         "data_type": def_.get("data_type", "TEXT"),
 517 |                         "widget_type": def_.get("widget_type", "INPUT"),
 518 |                         "is_required": def_.get("is_required", False),
 519 |                         "is_unique": def_.get("is_unique", False),
 520 |                         "is_system": True, # Always system
 521 |                         "is_active": True,
 522 |                         "read_only": True, # Immutable
 523 |                         "configuration": def_.get("configuration", {}),
 524 |                         "is_dynamic": False
 525 |                     }
 526 |                 logger.debug(f"   â†³ [Schema] Static Fields Loaded: {len(fields)}")
 527 | 
 528 |             # 2. FETCH DYNAMIC SCHEMA (The Overlay)
 529 |             logger.debug(f"   â†³ [Schema] Querying Dynamic Attributes...")
 530 | 
 531 |             # Use local method to avoid circular dependency issues
 532 |             dynamic_attributes = await MetaService.get_attributes(db, domain, active_only=active_only)
 533 |             
 534 |             for attr in dynamic_attributes:
 535 |                 # Dynamic overrides Static if key matches
 536 |                 fields[attr.key] = {
 537 |                     "id": attr.id,
 538 |                     "key": attr.key,
 539 |                     "label": attr.label,
 540 |                     "description": attr.description,
 541 |                     "data_type": attr.data_type,
 542 |                     "widget_type": attr.widget_type,
 543 |                     "is_required": attr.is_required,
 544 |                     "is_unique": attr.is_unique,
 545 |                     "is_system": attr.is_system,
 546 |                     "is_active": attr.is_active,
 547 |                     "read_only": attr.is_system, 
 548 |                     "configuration": attr.configuration,
 549 |                     "is_dynamic": True
 550 |                 }
 551 |             logger.debug(f"   â†³ [Schema] Dynamic Attributes Merged: {len(dynamic_attributes)}")
 552 |                 
 553 |             return {"domain": domain, "fields": fields}
 554 | 
 555 |         except Exception as e:
 556 |             logger.error(f"ðŸ”¥ [Schema] CRASH in get_fused_schema({domain}): {e}", exc_info=True)
 557 |             # Return empty schema instead of crashing, allowing UI to recover
 558 |             return {"domain": domain, "fields": {}, "error": str(e)}
 559 | 
 560 |     @staticmethod
 561 |     async def invalidate_cache(domain: str):
 562 |         logger.info(f"ðŸ”¥ [CACHE] Invalidated for Domain: {domain}")

 175 | 
 176 | class SystemConfig(Base):
 177 |     """
 178 |     THE CONTROL KNOBS.
 179 |     A typed Key-Value store for Runtime Configuration (Feature Flags, Limits).
 180 |     """
 181 |     __tablename__ = "system_config"
 182 | 
 183 |     id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)
 184 |     
 185 |     # Identity
 186 |     key = Column(String(100), nullable=False, unique=True, index=True)
 187 |     label = Column(String(255), nullable=False)
 188 |     description = Column(String(500), nullable=True)
 189 | 
 190 |     # Value Handling
 191 |     value_type = Column(String(20), nullable=False, default="STRING") # STRING, BOOLEAN, NUMBER, JSON
 192 |     value_raw = Column(Text, nullable=True) # Stores the actual value as string
 193 |     
 194 |     # Scope
 195 |     category = Column(String(50), default="GENERAL", index=True) # SECURITY, AI, UX
 196 |     is_encrypted = Column(Boolean, default=False) # If true, value is encrypted
 197 |     is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
 198 |     
 199 |     # Audit
 200 |     created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
 201 |     updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
 202 | 
 203 |     def __repr__(self):
 204 |         return f"<SystemConfig(key='{self.key}', type='{self.value_type}')>"
 205 | 
 206 |     @property
 207 |     def typed_value(self):
 208 |         """
 209 |         @description: Auto-converts value_raw based on value_type.
 210 |         """
 211 |         if self.value_raw is None: return None
 212 |         
 213 |         if self.value_type == "BOOLEAN":
 214 |             return self.value_raw.lower() in ('true', '1', 'yes', 'on')
 215 |         if self.value_type == "NUMBER":
 216 |             try:
 217 |                 return float(self.value_raw) if '.' in self.value_raw else int(self.value_raw)
 218 |             except ValueError:
 219 |                 return 0
 220 |         if self.value_type == "JSON":
 221 |             import json
 222 |             try:
 223 |                 return json.loads(self.value_raw)
 224 |             except:
 225 |                 return {}
 226 |         return self.value_raw
 227 |
