 230 | #  3. HYPERVISOR CONTROL CIRCUIT (The Level 9 Switchboard)
 231 | # ==============================================================================
 232 | 
 233 | class CircuitBreaker(Base):
 234 |     """
 235 |     The System Hypervisor's Memory.
 236 |     Controls the operational state of every moving part in the OS.
 237 |     """
 238 |     __tablename__ = "sys_circuit_breakers"
 239 | 
 240 |     id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)
 241 | 
 242 |     # WHAT are we controlling? (The URI)
 243 |     # Format: "domain:USER", "scope:USER:SIGNUP", "system:MAINTENANCE"
 244 |     target = Column(String(150), nullable=False, index=True)
 245 | 
 246 |     # WHICH Plane? (The Aspect)
 247 |     # Values: 'UI', 'API', 'WORKER', 'DATA'
 248 |     plane = Column(String(20), nullable=False, index=True)
 249 | 
 250 |     # THE STATE
 251 |     # Values: 'NOMINAL' (On), 'HALTED' (Off), 'DEGRADED' (ReadOnly), 'MAINTENANCE'
 252 |     status = Column(String(20), nullable=False, default="NOMINAL")
 253 |     
 254 |     # EXTENSIBILITY: Links to Module Registry Types
 255 |     module_type = Column(String(50), nullable=True) # e.g. 'WIZARD', 'JOB'
 256 | 
 257 |     # AUDIT
 258 |     updated_by = Column(String(100), nullable=True)
 259 |     reason = Column(String(255), nullable=True)
 260 |     updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now(), server_default=func.now())
 261 | 
 262 |     # Constraints: One switch per plane per target
 263 |     __table_args__ = (
 264 |         UniqueConstraint('target', 'plane', name='uq_circuit_target_plane'),
 265 |     )
 266 | 
 267 |     def __repr__(self):
 268 |         return f"<CircuitBreaker(target='{self.target}', plane='{self.plane}', status='{self.status}')>"

  49 | async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
  50 |     logger.info("ðŸš€ [Flodock] Platform Starting...")
  51 |     LogicInterceptor.register(Session)
  52 |     
  53 |     # âš¡ PHASE 1: KERNEL BOOT (Read-Only Cache Hydration)
  54 |     async with AsyncSessionLocal() as session:
  55 |         try:
  56 |             logger.info("ðŸ”® [Kernel] Hydrating System Registry from Database...")
  57 |             # âš¡ ARCHITECTURAL INVARIANT: The API Server only READS during boot.
  58 |             # Seeding is strictly delegated to the standalone `seed.py` Orchestrator.
  59 |             await domain_registry.refresh_from_db(session)
  60 |             
  61 |             logger.info("âœ¨ [Kernel] System Registry Synchronized.")
  62 |         except Exception as e:
  63 |             logger.critical(f"ðŸ”¥ [Kernel] BOOT FAILURE: {e}", exc_info=True)
  64 |             # We don't raise here to allow the API to start in "Safe Mode" if DB fails,
  65 |             # but in Level 100 we might want to crash. For now, we log loud.
  66 |     
  67 |     yield
  68 |     logger.info("ðŸ›‘ [Flodock] Platform Shutting Down...")
  69 |     await engine.dispose()
  70 | 
  71 | def create_application() -> FastAPI:
  72 |     application = FastAPI(
  73 |         title=settings.PROJECT_NAME,
  74 |         version=settings.VERSION,
  75 |         openapi_url=f"{settings.API_V1_STR}/openapi.json",
  76 |         lifespan=lifespan,
  77 |         docs_url="/docs",
  78 |         redoc_url="/redoc",
  79 |     )
  80 | 
  81 |     # âš¡ GLOBAL INTERCEPTOR (Business Logic Gates)
  82 |     @application.middleware("http")
  83 |     async def global_interceptor(request: Request, call_next):
  84 |         start_time = time.time()
  85 |         path = request.url.path
  86 |         method = request.method
  87 |         
  88 |         # 1. MAINTENANCE CHECK (Global)
  89 |         if not path.startswith(("/docs", "/openapi.json", "/api/v1/system")):
  90 |             async with AsyncSessionLocal() as db:
  91 |                 result = await db.execute(select(SystemConfig.value_raw).where(SystemConfig.key == "MAINTENANCE_MODE"))
  92 |                 mode = result.scalar()
  93 |                 if mode and mode.lower() in ('true', '1', 'on'):
  94 |                     return JSONResponse(status_code=503, content={"error": "System Maintenance", "detail": "Platform Offline"})
  95 | 
  96 |         # 2. âš¡ DOMAIN ENFORCEMENT (Kill Switch)
  97 |         allowed, reason = await DomainEnforcer.is_api_allowed(path)
  98 |         if not allowed:
  99 |             logger.warning(f"ðŸ›¡ï¸ [Enforcer] BLOCKED {method} {path} - Reason: {reason}")
 100 |             return JSONResponse(
 101 |                 status_code=403, 
 102 |                 content={"error": "Access Denied", "detail": reason, "domain_lock": True}
 103 |             )
 104 | 
 105 |         try:
 106 |             response = await call_next(request)
 107 |             return response
 108 |         except Exception as e:
 109 |             process_time = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
 110 |             logger.critical(f"ðŸ’¥ CRITICAL FAILURE: {method} {path} - {process_time:.2f}ms", exc_info=True)
 111 |             return JSONResponse(status_code=500, content={"error": "Internal Kernel Panic", "detail": str(e)})
 112 | 
 113 |     # âš¡ INFRASTRUCTURE MIDDLEWARE (Execution Order: Bottom-Up)
 114 |     
 115 |     # 3. CORS (Outermost)
 116 |     application.add_middleware(
 117 |         CORSMiddleware,
 118 |         allow_origins=[str(origin) for origin in settings.BACKEND_CORS_ORIGINS],
 119 |         allow_credentials=True,
 120 |         allow_methods=["*"],
 121 |         allow_headers=["*"],
 122 |     )
 123 | 
 124 |     # 2. CONTEXT HYDRATION (Injects User/TraceID)
 125 |     application.add_middleware(ContextMiddleware)
 126 | 
 127 |     # 1. ROUTER MOUNTING
 128 |     load_domains(application)
 129 |     application.include_router(meta_router, prefix="/api/v1/meta", tags=["Meta-Kernel"])
 130 |     application.include_router(system_router, prefix="/api/v1/system", tags=["System-Core"])
 131 |     application.include_router(resource_router, prefix="/api/v1/resource", tags=["Universal-Resource"])
 132 |     application.include_router(workflow_router, prefix="/api/v1", tags=["Workflow-Engine"])
 133 |     application.include_router(ai_router, prefix="/api/v1/ai", tags=["AI-Cortex"])
 134 |     
 135 |     return application
 136 | 
 137 | app = create_application()

 504 |       * **1.** RESOLVE METADATA
 505 |       * **2.** RESOLVE CONTEXT
 506 |       * We grab the Trace ID from the request context to link API logs with Kafka logs
 507 |       * **3.** RESOLVE PARTITION KEY (Critical for Kafka)
 508 |       * If not provided, we try to use entity_id. If that's missing, we fallback to "global".
 509 |       * **WARNING:** "global" puts everything on one partition (ordering guaranteed but low throughput).
 510 |       * **4.** ENVELOPE CONSTRUCTION
 511 |       * **5.** WRITE TO OUTBOX
 512 |       * In Level 100, we DO raise. If the event cannot be logged, the transaction is unsafe.
 513 | 
 514 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`commit`**
 515 |       > *Finalizes the transaction.*
 516 |

 781 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/meta/engine.py`
 782 | **Components & Logic:**
 783 | 
 784 | - ðŸ“¦ **`PolicyEngine`**
 785 |     > *The Universal Logic Executor.*
 786 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`evaluate`**
 787 |       > *The Main Entry Point.*
 788 |       * **1.** Prepare Data Context (Sandbox Envelope)
 789 |       * We wrap the data to allow 'context.meta' or 'context.actor' access if needed later.
 790 |       * Strategy: Pass object directly. Rules should be written as `host.weight > 10`.
 791 |       * **2.** Iterate Policies
 792 |       * **3.** Merge Results based on Governance Strategy
 793 |       * **4.** Apply Resolution Strategy ( The Judge )
 794 | 
 795 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_evaluate_single_policy`**
 796 |       > *Executes one Policy Bundle (which may contain multiple Rules).*
 797 |       * Policies store rules as a JSONB list: [{ "logic": "...", "action": "BLOCK", ... }]
 798 |       * A. Execute JMESPath
 799 |       * Boolean expressions: `host.age > 18` returns True/False.
 800 |       * B. Handle Match (Triggered)
 801 |       * âš¡ RESOLVE DYNAMIC VALUES
 802 |       * If action involves data, we must check if the value is a reference (e.g. actor.id)
 803 |       * **SAFEGUARD:** Bad rule syntax should not crash the system.
 804 |       * âš¡ FAIL OPEN: Treat crash as WARNING, not BLOCK.
 805 | 
 806 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_resolve_value`**
 807 |       > *Detects if a value is a reference (e.g. 'actor.id') and resolves it against the context.*
 808 |       * Heuristic: If it looks like a known context path, try to resolve it.
 809 |       * This matches the 'Value Source' logic in the Frontend Policy Editor.
 810 |       * If resolution works, return it. If it returns None, it might mean the field is missing,
 811 |       * but we return None rather than the string literal "actor.id".
 812 |       * If JMESPath crashes, fallback to the string literal
 813 | 
 814 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_apply_strategy`**
 815 |       > *Decides the final outcome based on the strategy.*
 816 |       * Default: Any violation kills the transaction
 817 |       * If (Total - Violations) > 0, then Pass.
 818 | 
 819 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_serialize`**
 820 |       > *Helper to convert SQLAlchemy objects to Dict for JMESPath.*
 821 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_log_summary`**
 822 |

 864 | 
 865 | - ðŸ“¦ **`XStateInterpreter`**
 866 |     > *A lightweight, fault-tolerant interpreter for XState v5 definitions.*
 867 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`__init__`**
 868 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`get_initial_state`**
 869 |       > *Returns the starting state of the machine.*

 871 |       > *Determines the next state based on the current state and the incoming event.*
 872 |       * **1.** Validate Current State
 873 |       * **2.** Look for Transitions ('on' block)
 874 |       * **3.** Match Event
 875 |       * XState allows 'on': { "EVENT": "TARGET" } OR 'on': { "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET" } }
 876 |       * **4.** Resolve Target
 877 |       * Short syntax: "EVENT": "TARGET"
 878 |       * Object syntax: "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET", "actions": [...] }
 879 |       * Array syntax (Guards): "EVENT": [{ "target": "T1", "guard": "cond" }]
 880 |       * For Phase 1, we just take the first unconditional match or the first one.

1348 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/utilities/async_bridge.py`
1349 | **Components & Logic:**
1350 | 
1351 | - ðŸ“¦ **`AsyncBridge`**
1352 |     > *The Connector between the Blocking DB Layer and the Non-Blocking Logic Layer.*
1353 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`run_sync`**
1354 |       > *Executes a coroutine synchronously by spawning a fresh Event Loop in a separate thread.*
1355 |       * âš¡ 1. CAPTURE CONTEXT
1356 |       * Snapshot the current state (User, Request ID, etc.)
1357 |       * This allows the background thread to "know" who initiated the save.
1358 |       * âš¡ 2. SETUP SIDECAR LOOP
1359 |       * âš¡ 3. EXECUTE WITHIN CONTEXT
1360 |       * We wrap the execution in ctx.run() so the coroutine sees the vars.
1361 |       * Note: We must wrap the loop.run_until_complete call itself,
1362 |       * or create a wrapper task that runs in context.
1363 |       * Best practice: ctx.run(task)
1364 |       * The loop itself doesn't need the context, the coroutine does.
1365 |       * However, ctx.run() takes a callable.
1366 |       * We simply run the loop logic.
1367 |       * This ensures the async task inherits the context
1368 |       * But simpler: we just run the whole block in context if possible.
1369 |       * Actually, contextvars context applies to the *thread* execution stack.
1370 |       * So executing ctx.run(func) sets the context for 'func'.
1371 |       * âš¡ 4. SPAWN THREAD WITH CONTEXT
1372 |       * We pass 'target' to ctx.run, so 'target' runs with the variables set.
1373 |       * But we are starting a NEW thread. ctx.run() only works in the CURRENT thread.
1374 |       * To pass context to a NEW thread, we must run ctx.run INSIDE the new thread.
1375 |       * "Re-hydrate" the context inside the new thread
1376 |       * Block until the Sidecar finishes (Gatekeeper behavior)
1377 | 
1378 |

1380 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/utils/reflection.py`
1381 | **Components & Logic:**
1382 | 
1383 | - Æ’ **`reflect_model_schema`**
1384 |     > *Introspects a SQLAlchemy Model and returns a structured Context Graph.*
1385 |     * Indentation for logging readability
1386 |     * **1.** SCALAR FIELDS
1387 |     * âš¡ ARCHITECTURAL INVARIANT: Skip Dynamic Containers
1388 |     * The bucket itself is not a field, it holds the fields.
1389 |     * --- A. Type Mapping ---
1390 |     * Map SQLAlchemy Types to UI Types
1391 |     * --- B. Metadata Extraction (The Explicit Strategy) ---
1392 |     * We look for the 'info' dict on the column definition first.
1393 |     * Fallback to Heuristics if missing.
1394 |     * Label: Override or Auto-Generate
1395 |     * System/Read-Only Status
1396 |     * **1.** Explicit Override
1397 |     * **2.** Heuristic Fallback (Safety Net)
1398 |     * Final Decision Logic
1399 |     * Special Case: 'hashed_password'
1400 |     * Should be "password" widget, but never readable.
1401 |     * --- C. Construct Field Definition ---
1402 |     * Alias for logic engine
1403 |     * Placeholder for extended config
1404 |     * Inject options if found via Enum or Info
1405 |     * **2.** RELATIONSHIPS (The Graph)
1406 |     * Only recurse if we haven't hit the limit
1407 |     * Determine Cardinality
1408 |     * Recursive Call
1409 |     * **3.** CONSTRUCT OUTPUT

2049 |     * --- RESET MODE (Reverse Waves) ---
2050 |     * âš¡ PHASE 0.5: KERNEL HYDRATION
2051 |     * --- SEED MODE (Forward Waves) ---
2052 |     * Guard: Don't run History in Prod unless explicit
2053 | 
2054 | - Æ’ **`main`**
2055 |

2061 |     * **1.** Ensure it exists (Prime the cache/db)
2062 |     * **2.** Toggle State (The Mutation)
2063 |     * This calls the refactored ORM method

4542 | ### ðŸ“„ `LogicEngine.ts`
4543 | > A lightweight parser for conditional rendering strings (e.g. "host.role == 'admin'").
4544 | 
4545 | | Attribute | Value |
4546 | | :--- | :--- |
4547 | | **security-level** | `LEVEL 9 (Sandboxed Evaluation)` |
4548 | | **invariant** | `Evaluation must never crash the UI, even with invalid syntax.` |
4549 | | **narrator** | `Logs evaluation trace to F12.` |
4550 | 
4551 | **Components & Logic:**
4552 | 
4553 | * **`LogicEngine`**
4554 |   * **Logic Flow:**
4555 |     * `Regex to find "host.xyz" or "formData.xyz"`
4556 |     * `Captures 'xyz'`
4557 |     * `logger.trace("LOGIC", `ðŸ” Analyzed dependencies for "${expression}"`, { deps });`
4558 |     * `1. Trivial Cases`
4559 |     * `2. Prepare Sandbox`
4560 |     * `We map 'host' and 'formData' to the same context for convenience`
4561 |     * `Helper for simple "contains" checks`
4562 |     * `3. Execution`
4563 |     * `ðŸ›¡ï¸ SECURITY: Function constructor is safer than eval(), but still requires`
4564 |     * `strict input sanitization. In a Level 9 system, we'd use a parser (AST).`
4565 |     * `For now, we wrap in a try-catch sandbox.`
4566 |     * `Allow-list check (Basic prevention of window/alert access)`
4567 |     * `logger.trace("LOGIC", `âš¡ Evaluated: "${expression}"`, { result, context_sample: Object.keys(context) });`
4568 |     * `Fail Open or Closed?`
4569 |     * `For visibility (show_if), we fail CLOSED (hide it) to prevent broken UI.`
4570 |     * `For requirements (required_if), we fail OPEN (not required) to prevent blocking.`
